Notes

- Tests and `scripts/` were excluded from usage checks.
- Next.js `app/` and `pages/` files are treated as entrypoints; all exports in those files are assumed used to avoid false positives.
- Path alias imports (tsconfig paths) are not fully resolved; some items may be false positives.
- Unreachable code detection is heuristic (e.g., literal `if (false)` or immediate statements after `return`).
- Items marked “Referenced in docs/comments” are flagged but not recommended for removal.
